The lowland hiking are along the lake isn't really anything and it doesn't circle the lake so don't try. You really got to go up the hill which it seems like there's an easier but longer route or a more direct and steeper route from the front. If you plan to go up the hill which it doesn't seem hardly any people do then plan to spend at least 3 hours. Trail paths are wide and unpaved so plan on being muddy after rain. There's 1 porta potty at the small parking lot which is often quickly filled then blocked from the entrance. Main parking is way back towards the rose garden which is under renovation.<//Review>

<review>I‚Äôve been here few times, and all were incredible enjoyable.
I came back today December/12/2020.
It is 6 miles loop and 1,257 feet of elevation gain.
The trail is started at Grant lake parking.
My loop started with Yerba Buena Trail, Canada De. Pala Trail, los Huecis Trail , Halls Valley Trail, and back to the parking lot.
There is not really any shade. Stunning views, and a great workout.
Not sure if I want to share this gem with everyone, but with all that is going on, we can all use a little more happiness. This is an awesome park if you want to hike in solitude.
The trail got rebuilt after the fire, very new, wide and rolling, no cows, very low foot traffic.
Everyone has more room to improvement, you won‚Äôt disappointed when you get up to the top of the hill. I‚Äôm looking forward to going back.< /review>< pics>
